beures captaine towne would fall compoſition duke lorraine would compound without notwithſtanding truſtie knight lacked courage fell intreaties perſwaſions whereas mine opinion ſtouter language would better haue preuailed god already diſpoſed heerof towne held three day longer releeued conclude ſaid de beures agreed engliſh men yeelded place duke lorraine 3 ſo departed within bag baggage next day
